<h2><span id="English" class="mw-headline">English</span></h2>
<div style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;" class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright">

<h3><span id="Proper_noun" class="mw-headline">Proper noun</span></h3>
<p><strong lang="en" class="Latn headword">Wiktionary</strong> ‎(<i>plural</i> <span class="form-of lang-en proper-noun-plural-form-of"><b lang="en" class="Latn"><a title="Wiktionaries" href="/wiki/Wiktionaries#English">Wiktionaries</a></b></span>)</p>
<ol>
<li>A <a title="collaborative" href="/wiki/collaborative">collaborative</a> project run by the <a title="w:Wikimedia Foundation" class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikimedia_Foundation">Wikimedia Foundation</a> to produce a <a title="free" href="/wiki/free">free</a> and <a title="complete" href="/wiki/complete">complete</a> <a title="dictionary" href="/wiki/dictionary">dictionary</a> in every <a title="language" href="/wiki/language">language</a>.</li>
<li>The dictionaries, collectively, produced by that project.</li>
<li>A particular version of this dictionary project, written in a certain language, such as the English-language Wiktionary or simply the English Wiktionary.</li>
</ol>
<h4><span id="Quotations" class="mw-headline">Quotations</span></h4>
<p><span class="see-cites">For usage examples of this term, see <a title="Citations:Wiktionary" href="/wiki/Citations:Wiktionary#English">Citations:Wiktionary</a>.</span></p>
